 bhatkal va haddi ko enie ne guuruuvaar ko nepal seemaa se giraftaar kiya tha

 jail ke adhikariyon ne bataaya ki jail main donon raat bhar nahin soe
 "bhatkal and Akhtar were interrogated by a team of NIA officers at the highly secure military police camp in Patna," the official said
 " donon aatankiyon ko shuukravaar ko vishesh vimaan dwaara transit remand par dilli laayaa gaya
 Bhatkal was named in the Delhi Police's list of the 15 most wanted terrorists in the nationwide bombings, and police from 12 states were looking for Bhatkal in bomb blasts and terror attacks across the country
 bhatkal kii giraftaar ke saath hi enie ko ummid he ki vah iem se jude aatanki ghatnaon, aatankwaadiyon evam milane vaali vittiya madad kaa bhandaphod karne main kaamyaab hogi
 According to Nepal's leading newspaper 'kantipur', Bhatkal and Abdul Karim Tunda were arrested from Kathmandu and handed over to Indian authorities
 lekin nepal ke adhikariyon ne isse inkaar kiya he
 The newspaper claimed that Bhatkal was arrested from Kathmandu by Nepali intelligence agencies on Wednesday and then handed over to India on the Raxaul border of indo-nepal
 samachar patr ne yah bhi daawa kiya he ki 16 agast ko giraftaar kiye gaye aatankwaadi tunda ko bhi kathmandu ke barbazar main jama masjid se nikalate samay giraftaar kiya gaya tha
 Nepal's home ministry spokesman Shankar Prasad Koirala said he had no information about the arrests
 bhatkal par desh main 11 bade bam visphot main shaamil rahane kaa aarope he
 He is the prime suspect of the 2008 serial blasts in Connaught Place, Ghaffar Market and Greater Kailash areas of Delhi
 teen jagahon par hue visphoton main 26 log maare gaye the or 133 anya ghayal hue the

 9 <! - td {border: 1px solid # ccc;} br {mso-data-placement: same-cell;} -> Who were the candidates: Chatra Lok Sabha seat is one of the 14 Lok Sabha seats in Jharkhand
 is seat par sabaki najar thi
 The current BJP MP Sunil Kumar Singh and Subhash Prasad Yadav from RJD were in the fray here
 is seat se 17 nirdaleey samet kul 26 pratyaashee chunavi ran main utre the
 Chatra Lok Sabha seat is the stronghold of Lalu Yadav's Rashtriya Janata Dal (RJD)
 yahaan argedy kaa muqabla bijepi ke sunil kumaar singh se he
 Sunil Kumar Singh is the sitting MP from here
 yah seat naksal prabhavit jilon palamu, chatra or lateher main faili hui he
 Last time, who won the BJP in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, the BJP won a historic victory in Chatra Lok Sabha seat in the Modi wave
 yahaan se bijepi ke sunil singh ne congress ke dhiraj sahu ko haraaya tha
 Sunil Singh had received 2 lakh 95 thousand votes, while Dheeraj Sahu had received one lakh 17 thousand votes
 tisare number par rahe trinmul congress ke naushaad alam ko kareeb 8 hajaar vot mili the
 Political background Vijaya Raje of Janata Party won this seat in 1957
 vijaya raaje 1962 or 1967 kaa chunaav bhi nirdaleey pratyaashee ke taur par jeet chuki hai
 In 1971, Shankar Dayal Singh of Congress won from this seat and in 1977 Sukhdev Verma of Janata Party won Parliament
 saal 1980 main congress ke ranjit singh jite the
 The elections of 1989 and 1991 were successful in winning Upendra Nath Verma on Janata Dal ticket
 saal 1996 main pehali baar is seat par bijepi kaa khaataa khulaa tha or uske tikat par dhirendra agarwal chunaav jite the
 The 1998 election was also won by Dhirendra Agarwal on a BJP ticket
 saal 1999 main is seat se argedy ke naagamani kushvaha jite the
 After this, in 2004, Dhirendra Agarwal became MP for the third time on RJD ticket
 iske baad saal 2009 main nirdaleey pratyaashee indra singh namdhari chunaav jite the
 In the 2014 elections, bjp's Sunil Kumar Singh won
 saamaajik tanabanachatra loksabhaa seat kii adhikansh aabaadi gaanvon main rahati he or isamen adhiktar anusuchit jati ke log shaamil he
 Apart from this, there is a good number of backward castes on this seat
 is seat ke tahat chatra (essi), latehar (essi), manika (asti), simriya (essi) or panki vidhansabha siten aati hai
 Chatra parliamentary constituency has five assembly seats
 inamen se teen anusuchit jati or ek anusuchit janajati ke liye arakshit he
 Apart from scheduled castes and tribes, the backward castes dominate the Chatra seat
 palamu, chatra or lateher jile jharkhand ke pichde jilon main se ek he

 arakshit rail tikaton kaa durupyog rokane or hastantarit tikat par yatra ke maamalon main kami laane ke uddeshy se rail mantralay ne 15 farvari se vaataanukoolit (asi) shrenee kii bogiyon main safar karne vaale yatriyon ke liye mul pahachaanapatr saath rakhana anivaary karne kaa nirnay liya he
 According to a Railway Ministry release, nine types of identity cards (original) are given to one of the passengers of the group of AC-3 tier, AC-2 tier, first class AC, AC chair car and one of the passengers who reserved seats in special category
 Have to keep one of them
 yatra ke dauraan pahachaanapatr maange jane par asi shrenee ke yatriyon ko mul pahachaanapatr prastut karnaa hoga
 In the event of non-submission of the original identity card, these passengers will be treated as un-ticketed and will be charged accordingly
 piares kanutor yaa ai-tikat dwaara arakshit asi shrenee ke tikaton kii kharid ke samay haalanki pahachaanapatr (mul yaa chhayaprati) kii aavashyaktaa nahin he
 In cases where passengers have been upgraded from Sleeper class to Air-conditioned class and also in cases in which they are upgraded in case of difference in the travel fare of the passenger by the ticket checking staff during the journey, There is no need to keep identity evidence during
 yah nayaa nirdesh pehle se maujuud nirdeshon ke atirikt hai, jiske tahat tatkaal tikat or i-tikat booking karaane vaale yatriyon ko yatra ke dauraan mul pahchaan patr apane paas rakhana hota he

 unhone kaha ki uttarapradesh ko adarsh pradesh banane ke liye bhaajapa kii sarkaar laana jaruri he
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) alpsankhyak kaary mantri ne kaha ki uttar pradesh ko 'mafiaraj, gundaraj, bhrashtachar ke gathbandhan' ke changul se chhudaa kar bhaajapa rajya ko vikaas, vishwaas, sushasan ke sankalp ke saath kaam karne vaali sarkaar degi
 The BJP believes in the 'draft of development' and not on 'deal of votes'
 unhone ne aarope lagaaya ki jahaan ek taraf congress 'beyimaanon kii benami property' ban gai he, jiske daravaaje par 'tu-let' kaa board laga hua he, duusari ore samaajawaadee party is benami property kii 'kiraayedaar' ban gai he
 Naqvi alleged that the BSP has become a 'habitation of musclemen and unscrupulous'
 kendriya mantri ne kaha ki bhaajapa 'bahubaliyon-beyimaanon kaa bantaadhaar' kar prachand bahumat se uttar pradesh main sarkaar banaaegi
 The BJP, which believes in 'inclusive development and trust', is the guarantee of the progress of all sections of society
 nakvi ne kaha ki gaanv, garib, kisaan, kamjor tabake, dalit, alpsankhyak, yuva or mahilaayein centre kii pradhanmantri narendra modi ke netritv vaali sarkaar ke har kalyankari yojana or kaarykram kaa centre bindu hai
 Our resolve is to bring 'happiness in the eyes of every poor and happiness in life'
 unhone kaha ki pradhanmantri modi kaa lakshya vikaas kii raushnee samaaj ke aakhri vyakti tak pahunchaana he
 Accusing parties like Congress, SP, BSP of indulging in politics of appeasement, Naqvi said that how 'empowerment without appeasement' has been done by bjp's central government
 bhaajapa sushasan kii baat karti he, 'samaveshi vikaas' kii baat karti he
 He said that the atmosphere of development and trust created by the Modi government in the country is not digesting those who have been 'politically exploiting' the poor and weaker sections for decades
 pradhanmantri modi ke vikaas ke kaaryon se desh bhar kii janata, uttar pradesh kii janata khush he, notebandi jaise faisle kaa samarthan kar rahi he jisase bhrashtachar, kaledhan ke khilaaf nirnaayak ladaai shuru hui he
 Taking a dig at the Congress and SP, he alleged that people who used to curse each other in the morning and evening just before the election was announced, held each other responsible for the state's misery, while people have become one today 
 vikaas or vishwaas ke maahaul se ye partiyaan itani dar gayi hai ki apni dashakon puraani dushmani bhula kar gale lag rahi hai
 The Union Minister said that the reality is that these parties are seen moving their land
 kisi kii cycle pankchar ho gai he, koi pankchar cycle kaa handle tham kar apni duubati naiya ko paar lagaana chahta he
 Naqvi appealed to the people to be part of the 'caravan of Good Governance and Development' in the mahaparva election of democracy
 bhaajapa ko janadesh den 
 This country, state, society will be good for everyone

 10-15 saal pehle 24 saal kii umr main raajnneeti main aayaa or bahut kuch seekhney ko mila
 He told the story of the temples saying that one was a priest of Congress and one was a priest of BJP
 pehla mandir
 Went to Shiva's temple and worshiped and asked Panditji what you did
 doodh daalaa, pani daalaa aapane kiya kya
 The priest said that i am not from here but i belong to Kashmir, but do not tell anyone, where you will see God will be seen there
 ab hamen jo karnaa he karne de
 Referring to the second temple, he said that he asked the priest again there but the priest said that the son should not ask now
 maine puja kar di he or tum piem banane ja rahe ho, lekin piem banane ke baad mandir ke chat par sona laga dena
 Meaning a person tells the truth, so the Congress tells the truth
 unhone duusare mandir kii tulana bijepi se kii or kaha ki wo nafrat failaate hai, lekin congress nafrat nahin karti he
 Rahul Gandhi said that today the country is in difficulty
 kisaan kehete hai ham ji nahin sakate hai
 There is no money in farming, so suicide has to be done
 unhone kaha ki desh main yuva berogaar baithe hai
 The trust he placed on PM Modi has been broken
 ab yuva sawaal puch rahe hai ki rojgaar kab milegaa
 How will this problem be solved? puure desh main congress hi ek sanghathan he jo yuvaaon ko rojgaar de saktaa he, lekin is kaam ko puraa karne ke liye sanghathan badalanaa padegaa
 Rahul Gandhi said that youth have energy, power to change the country, but there is a wall between them and our leaders, so my job will be to break the wall
 lekin gusse se nahin pyaar se
 The wall has different forms
 parachute se tikat lekar girtaa he or kaaryakartaaon se kaha jaataa he ki tum kaaryakarta ho
 But i want to say that the workers will get tickets, this is what we did in Gujarat
 duusari diwaar ke bare me rahul ne kaha ki rajaneta or yuvaaon ke bich main diwaar he
 Four years ago, the youth thought that by voting for Modi ji, they would change the country, but Modi ji flew away
 ek taraf lalit modi or duusari taraf neerav modi
 The youth kept watching
 unhone kaha ki yuvaaon ke liye maine is stage ko khaali kiya he
 We will give opportunity to the youth
 hidustan ko badalanaa he to yuva hi badal saktaa he
 The country cannot be changed without youth, so i have vacated this stage
 jinke andar congress kii aag jalati he main unako kahana chahta hum ki talented ladke-ladakiyon ko yahaan laaungaa
 Referring to Mahatma Gandhi, Jawaharlal Nehru, Patel, Azad, Rahul said that any of these people could have awakened the country
 thik waisi hi congress party main dekhnaa chahta hum
 All youth will get a place in Congress
 duniya main aaj do vijan dikhaai de rahe hai, america or china ke bich main india kaa vijan aa jaae or duniya kahe ki yah vijan sabase acha he
 Compete with China, but have to compete with love
 hindustan main urja kii kami nahin he
 Congress party will work to add skill structure in every district
 kisaan kii fasal zyada se zyada kharaab ho jaati he
 The Congress will set up food processing factories across the country and protect farmers
 kisaanon ne desh ko banaaya he
 This country will never forget that
 congress dil se kisaanon kii raksha karegi
 Farmers will not back down from helping when needed
 congress sabaki party he
 Today Vyapam scam is being spread across the country
 yuva dharna de rahe hai

 congress desh kii shiksha vyavastha ko badalegi

 lekin yah log nahin maanenge

 bijepi ke log apni galati nahin maanenge

 lekin congress sachai ke saath khadi he

 isliye congress kii ladaai pandavon kii tarah he

 unhone gandhi kaa bhi zikr kiya or kaha ki unhone desh ke liye apni jaan de di

 He said that this is the truth of India that the youth here are unemployed
 unhone china kaa zikr karte hue kaha ki china aaj har jagah hai chaahe wo koi dukaan ho, doklam ho yaa pakistan har jagah china kaa varchasv he

 pradhanmantri narendra modi aaj rashtriya rajdhani ke indira gandhi stadium main pratham 'khelo india skool games' kaarykram kaa shubharambh karenge
 The objective of the 'khelo India' program is to revive the sports culture at the grassroots level
 iske liye desh main khele jane vaale sabhi khelon ke liye ek majboot sanrachana kaa nirmaan kiya jayega taaki bharat khelon main ek agrani raashtra ke rup main sthapit ho sake
 In keeping with the vision of Prime Minister Modi, 'khelo India School Games' will identify youth sports talent and help them develop as future champions
 ek ucch stareey samiti yuva khel pratibhaaon kii pahchaan karegi or unhen aath saalon tak paanch lakh rupee prativarsh kii aarthik sahaayta di jaaegi
 'khelo India' will be organized in the national capital from 31 January to 8 February
 17 varsh se kam umr ke yuva 16 khelon teerandaji, athletics, badminton, basketball, mukkebaaji, footbal, jimnastics, hockey, judo, kabddi, kho-kho, nishanebaaji, tairaaki, wolibal, bharottolan, kushti main hissaa lenge

 'khelo India' will be organized in the national capital from 31 January to 8 February
 17 varsh se kam umr ke yuva 16 khelon teerandaji, athletics, badminton, basketball, mukkebaaji, footbal, jimnastics, hockey, judo, kabddi, kho-kho, nishanebaaji, tairaaki, wolibal, bharottolan, kushti main hissaa lenge

 tippaniyan The 'khelo India School Games' will give 199 gold medals, 199 silver medals and 275 bronze medals
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 It is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) a high level committee will identify the youth sports talent and they will be given financial assistance of five lakh rupees per year for eight years
 'khelo india' kaa aayojan 31 janvari se 8 farvari tak rashtriya rajdhani main kiya jayega
 Youth under 17 will participate in 16 sports archery, athletics, badminton, basketball, boxing, football, gymnastics, hockey, judo, kabaddi, kho-kho, shooting, swimming, volleyball, weightlifting, wrestling
 is aayojan se bharat kii yuva khel pratibhaaen ubharkar saamne aaengi or isse desh kii khel shakti kaa bhi pataa chalegaa

 The Biju Janata Dal won this seat for the first time in 2014
 aazaadee ke baad shuruaati loksabhaa chunaav main yahaan congress kii badshahath rahi
 The Congress won the elections of 1951, 57 and 62
 1967 main sipiai ne is seat par apana khaataa kholaa or samarendra kundu vijayi hue 
 In 1971, the Congress returned here again
 1977 main indira virdohi lahar ke baad congress yahaan se haar gai or samarendra kundu ek baar phir se chunaav jite
 The Congress won the seat again in 1980 and 84
 1989 ke chunaav main samrendra kundu janata dal ke tikat par chunaav jite
 In 1991 and 96 this seat went to the Congress account
 atal-adwani ke daur main is seat camel khilaa
 In 1998, 99 and 2004, Kharbela Swain won elections on BJP ticket here
 2009 main bijedy or bijepi ke bich gathbandhan main hui tut kaa phayda congress ko mila or is seat se congress ke tikat par shrikant jena vijayi rahe
